<user_id>113775135883828002755<//user_id><name>Callan Koenig<//name>< Time>
1544034357667<//Time>
<Rate>3</Rate>< text>
With so many different Mexican options in Grand Central Market, it is difficult to choose which one to go to. Ana Maria's is a solid choice.

A good option if you are in a hurry since the line moves quickly and the folks behind the counter are helpful if you are unsure what to get. The portions, like most of the other taco stands in GCM, are large and can easily be used for multiple meals or shared among friends. They even give you extra tortillas!

I found the al pastor to be a bit dry but I went later in the day post the lunchtime rush. I may go again but with so many other places to try, it might be a while till I'm able to circle back.< /text>

<text>Ana Maria's will complete my Carnitas Tour of the Grand Central Market. I suppose I can go and conquer all the Chinese food now since they also seem to be in abundance here too. As per my usual Carnitas Journey rules, I got my burrito with all meat and no fillers like rice and beans. I did add onions and cilantro though for good measure.

Ana Maria's is located adjacent to Roasts To Go right smack dab in the middle of the market. I usually always get my burritos to go and end up eating at the outside benches. Ana Maria's can also be called a place with big-ass tacos as same as some of its neighbors. Tacos cost $2.50, but usually have so much meat crammed in there that they give you extra corn tortillas to make a second taco. Well, that's the next journey because this one is all about carnitas burritos.

-=- Carnitas Burrito, all meat -=- $5.50. This price ties for least expensive. The size of the burrito seems to suffer a bit though, but keep in mind that you will still be stuffed. Carnitas wasn't the juiciest of the bunch but it was still satisfying after drenching it with salsa. In the tortilla department, nothing special. It wasn't toasted or grilled in a way that helped the flavor. A good buttering or crisp usually gets my favor, but sadly not here. They give you plenty of lime wedges. I just squeezed all mine into my salsas since they were all going on there anyway.

For the sauces, I can say that the red sauce goes down like tomato sauce, the kick comes after. It's pretty runny and the least thick, but that kick was something different than the rest. I did prefer the green sauce though since you get the same kick, but with better flavor.</text><Pics>None</Pics><response>None<//response>< gmap_id>

< Text>
####UPDATED #### 3/18/2021

I have been to Spa many times after I wrote my previous review. They have been very kind to me. Their facials have done wonders on my skin.

Visiting the spa in general makes me happy. It smells so good in there and music is very relaxing. I am curious to try their body wrap in the future. Their shop has really great products which you may not be able to find else where. Do check it out if you ever plan to visit it. Don't forget to taste their apple cider , it's yummm :)

Overall, Its a very clean place. They are taking all the required precautions. I highly highly recommend this Spa especially for facials and massages.

-----------------------------------------------------------------

I have been to this spa several times and it has always been a good experience.  But TODAY wasn't. Last time, I had a facial and their esthetician ( Jessica ) did really great job with extracting my pimples and cleaning out the gunk. However, when I visited the spa after reopening my experience wasn't the same. I booked a facial as always and esthetician (a new one ) asked which kind of facial I would like to go for and I told her to do usual one (acne facial) and she did it. There was NO EXTRACTION in the process which was very very weird. I had a few breakouts when I went there and she dint even touch them and facial was for 110$ so I kind of felt like it was waste go money. Also, I DO NOT like the way they try to forcefully sell the MURAD products in the end. I already have a skincare routine and I know my skin needs and everybody does ;so making a suggestion is okay but forcing it is weird. Maybe just next time I will tell them before hand to include extraction in the acne facial.
